style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">WINNEBAGO INDUSTRIES ANNOUNCES FIRST QUARTER FISCAL 2020 RESULTS</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;font-weight:bold;">-- Strong Sales Growth Continues to Outperform the RV Industry --</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;font-weight:bold;">-- Reported Quarterly Diluted EPS of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;font-weight:bold;">$0.44</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;font-weight:bold;">, Adjusted EPS of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;font-weight:bold;">$0.73</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;font-weight:bold;">&#32;Up 4.3% Over Prior Year --</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;font-weight:bold;">-- Strong Operating Cash Flow of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;font-weight:bold;">$79.0 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;font-weight:bold;">, Up </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;font-weight:bold;">46%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;font-weight:bold;">&#32;Over Prior Year --</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;font-weight:bold;">-- Expanded Portfolio of Premier Brands With The Acquisition of Newmar --</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">FOREST CITY, IOWA, </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">December&#160;20, 2019</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;- Winnebago Industries, Inc. (NYSE:WGO), a leading outdoor lifestyle product manufacturer, today reported financial results for the Company's </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">first</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;quarter Fiscal </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">2020</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;text-decoration:underline;">First</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;text-decoration:underline;">&#32;Quarter Fiscal </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;text-decoration:underline;">2020</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;text-decoration:underline;">&#32;Results</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">Revenues for the Fiscal </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">2020</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">first</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;quarter ended </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">November&#160;30, 2019</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">, were </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$588.5 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">, an increase of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">19.2%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;compared to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$493.6 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;for the Fiscal </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">2019</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;period. Revenues excluding the recently acquired Newmar business were $552.8 million, representing an organic growth rate of 12.0% over the prior year period driven by strong growth in the Towable segment and modest growth in the Motorhome business. Gross profit was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$78.6 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">, an increase of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">10.7%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;compared to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$71.0 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;for the Fiscal </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">2019</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;period. Gross profit margin decreased </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">100</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;basis points in the quarter primarily due to a change in mix as a result of the acquisition of Newmar and the impact of the associated purchase accounting. Operating income was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$23.9 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;for the quarter, which includes $10.0 million of transaction costs related to the acquisition of Newmar, compared to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$32.6 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;in the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">first</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;quarter of last year. Fiscal </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">2020</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">first</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;quarter net income was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$14.1 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">, a decrease of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">36.5%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;compared to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$22.2 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;in the same period last year. Reported earnings per diluted share were </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$0.44</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">, a decrease of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">37.1%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;compared to reported earnings per diluted share of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$0.70</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;in the same period last year. Consolidated adjusted earnings per share were </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$0.73</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;for the first quarter, an increase of 4.3% over the prior period, excluding approximately $12.1 million, or $0.29 per share after tax, of transaction costs, inventory step-up, and the non-cash portion of the interest expense related to the convertible bond that was issued to finance the Newmar acquisition. Consolidated Adjusted EBITDA was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$42.0 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;for the quarter, an increase of 9.3% compared to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$38.5 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;last year.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">President and Chief Executive Officer Michael Happe commented, &#8220;We delivered strong consolidated results for the first quarter of Fiscal 2020 as we continued to make progress in transforming Winnebago Industries into a premier outdoor lifestyle company. Overall revenue growth remains strong, driven by vibrant Class B sales in our Motorhome segment and another stellar quarter from Grand Design in the Towable segment. These businesses are driving significant market share gains in the RV industry. Our RV retail market share is now 10.8% on a trailing three month basis through October, up 1.7 share points over the prior year period and exceeding our 2020 goal of 10% we established in November, 2017. Our results included approximately three weeks of contribution from the recently acquired Newmar business, the foremost luxury motorhome manufacturer in North America. We are extremely focused on the integration of the Newmar business and ensuring a smooth transition for Newmar's employees, dealers, and end-customers. Our continued growth reflects our competitive position in the RV industry and the resilience of our </font></div><div><br></div><div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">1</font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div><br></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">diversified portfolio, which has positioned us well to deliver solid results despite prevailing industry headwinds. As we look ahead to the balance of Fiscal 2020, we remain focused on authentically differentiating ourselves from the competition around quality, customer service and innovation. I want to thank all of our Winnebago Industries employees for their hard work during the quarter and for their unwavering commitment to our ambitious goal of transforming Winnebago Industries into a stronger enterprise. I also want to welcome the Newmar employees to the Winnebago Industries family and thank them for their hard work now and into the future as the integration process ramps up.&#8221; </font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;text-decoration:underline;">Towable</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">Revenues for the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">Towable</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;segment were </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$341.3 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;for the first quarter, up </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">16.5%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;over the prior year, driven by strong unit growth in the Grand Design RV product line. Segment Adjusted EBITDA was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$35.8 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">, up </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">16.1%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;over the prior year. Adjusted EBITDA margin of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">10.5%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;was in line with the prior period. Backlog decreased 22.0%, in units, compared to the prior year period reflecting an increased utilization of incremental capacity and a change in dealer ordering patterns to smaller and more frequent purchases.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;text-decoration:underline;">Motorhome</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">In the first quarter, revenues for the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">Motorhome</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;segment were </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$225.9 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">, up </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">24.6%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;from the prior year primarily driven by strength in the Class B line-up and the addition of Newmar revenues during the quarter. Excluding Newmar, segment revenues grew 4.9% over the prior year period. Segment Adjusted EBITDA was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$9.3 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">, down </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">22.1%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">, due to an unfavorable mix and higher SG&amp;A expense partially offset by the three week contribution to Adjusted EBITDA from the Newmar acquisition and pricing in excess of inflation. Adjusted EBITDA margin decreased </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">250</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;basis points. Backlog increased 34.2%, in units, compared to the prior year, due to the acquisition of Newmar and new product introductions in the Winnebago motorhome line-up, partially offset by a change in dealer ordering patterns to smaller and more frequent purchases.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;text-decoration:underline;">Balance Sheet and Cash Flow</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">As of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">November&#160;30, 2019</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">, the Company had total outstanding debt of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$463.5 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;(</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$560.0 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;of debt, net of convertible note discount of $84.0 million, and debt issuance costs of $12.5 million) and working capital of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$297.8 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">. Cash flow from operations was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$79.0 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;in the first quarter of Fiscal </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">2020</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">, reflecting a strong increase of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">45.9%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$24.9 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">, from the same period in Fiscal 2019.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;text-decoration:underline;">Quarterly Cash Dividend</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font directors approved a quarterly cash dividend of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$0.11</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;per share payable on January 29, 2020, to common stockholders of record at the close of business on January 15, 2020.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font process to identify and prioritize the most relevant environmental, social and governance related topics and goals. Additionally, the Company&#8217;s board of directors approved the addition of Sara Armbruster as a member of its board of directors.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">Mr. Happe continued, &#8220;We are eager to build upon the tremendous progress we&#8217;ve made towards enhancing our position as a leader in premium outdoor lifestyle solutions. The acquisition of Newmar is pivotal in increasing our competitiveness and we are excited about the accretion Newmar brings to our portfolio - culturally, strategically and financially. We enter Fiscal 2020 with a stronger business that now includes four of the most iconic brands in the outdoor lifestyle arena - Winnebago, Grand Design, Newmar, and Chris-Craft. The benefits of having an expanded and more diversified product portfolio have translated to more consistent earnings results and are driving incremental growth and market share expansion in our business. We continue to </font></div><div><br></div><div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">2</font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div><br></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">monitor the health of the RV and marine channels and the confidence of consumers. By keeping our teams focused on delivering against our golden threads - superior quality, valued innovation, outstanding customer service - we are confident that Winnebago Industries will continue to outperform the marketplace and maximize value for our shareholders and customers in fiscal year 2020.&#8221;</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;text-decoration:underline;">Conference Call</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">Winnebago Industries, Inc. will discuss </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">first</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;quarter Fiscal </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">2020</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;earnings results during a conference call scheduled for 9:00 a.m. Central Time today. Members of the news media, investors and the general public are invited to access a live broadcast of the conference call via the Investor Relations page of the Company's website at http://investor.wgo.net. The event will be archived and available for replay for the next 90 days.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;text-decoration:underline;">About Winnebago Industries</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">Winnebago Industries, Inc. is a leading U.S. manufacturer of outdoor lifestyle products under the Winnebago, Newmar, Grand Design, and Chris-Craft brands, which are used primarily in leisure travel and outdoor recreation activities. The Company builds quality motorhomes, travel trailers, fifth wheel products, and boats. Winnebago Industries has multiple facilities in Iowa, Indiana, Oregon, Minnesota, and Florida. The Company's common stock is listed on the New York Stock Exchange and trades under the symbol WGO. For access to Winnebago Industries' investor relations material or to add your name to an automatic email list for Company news releases, visit http://investor.wgo.net.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;text-decoration:underline;">Forward Looking Statements</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">This press release may contain forward-looking statements within the meaning of the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995. style="vertical-align:bottom;border-bottom:3px double #000000;background-color:#cceeff;padding-top:2px;padding-bottom:2px;"><div style="text-align:right;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">38,453</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:bottom;border-bottom:3px double #000000;background-color:#cceeff;"><div style="text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></td></tr></table></div></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">We have provided non-GAAP performance measures of Adjusted diluted income per share, EBITDA, and Adjusted EBITDA as comparable measures to illustrate the effect of non-recurring transactions occurring during the reported periods and improve comparability of our results from period to period. Adjusted diluted income per share is defined as income per share adjusted for items that impact the comparability of our results from period to period. EBITDA is defined as net income before interest expense, provision for income taxes, and depreciation and amortization expense. Adjusted EBITDA is defined as net income before interest expense, provision for income taxes, depreciation and amortization expense, and other adjustments made in order to present comparable results from period to period. We believe Adjusted diluted income per share and Adjusted EBITDA provides meaningful supplemental information about our operating performance because these measures exclude amounts that we do not consider part of our core operating results when assessing our performance. Examples of items excluded from Adjusted income per share include acquisition-related costs, acquisition-related fair-value inventory step-up, non-cash interest expense, and the tax impact of the adjustments. Examples of items excluded from Adjusted EBITDA include acquisition-related fair-value inventory step-up, acquisition-related costs, restructuring expenses, and non-operating income.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">Management uses these non-GAAP financial measures (a)&#160;to evaluate our historical and prospective financial performance and trends as well as our performance relative to competitors and peers; (b)&#160;to measure operational profitability on a consistent </font></div><div><br></div><div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">9</font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div><br></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">basis; (c) in presentations to the members of our board of directors to enable our board of directors to have the same measurement basis of operating performance as is used by management in its assessments of performance and in forecasting and budgeting for our company; (d) to evaluate potential acquisitions; and (e) to ensure compliance with covenants and restricted activities under the terms of our debt agreements. We believe these non-GAAP financial measures are frequently used by securities analysts, investors, and other interested parties to evaluate companies in our industry.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div><br></div><div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">10</font></div></div>	</div></body>
</html>
